The Special District Rickshaw Businessmen Held a General Meeting Yesterday to Establish a Cooperative for Manufacturing New Rickshaws

Nineteen Committee Members Elected to Prepare

Rickshaw Puller Registration to be Extended by Two Weeks

The rickshaw owners in the Special District of this city held a general meeting of all rickshaw owners at 9:00 AM yesterday at the Dashun Hall of the City Chamber of Commerce. More than 800 people, including Gu Songmao, Yin Zhiling, Hou Shao'an, Lu Dexin, Qiu Jixiang, Yin Zifang, and Jin Chunlin, attended. Yin Zhiling chaired the meeting and reported on the negotiations with the Rickshaw Committee and the correspondence. Then they began to discuss: (1) The ratification of the agreement and exchange of documents between the representatives of this association and the Municipal Council Rickshaw Committee. Resolved: Passed. (2) To prepare for the establishment of a temporary cooperative for manufacturing new rickshaws to standardize the rickshaw style. Resolved: Elected nineteen committee members. Resolved: Elected Gu Songmao, Yin Zhiling, Hou Shao'an, Liang Ruiting, Zhu Hegao, Lu Dexin, Qiu Jixiang, Jin Chunlin, Bao Zhenhuang, Xia Muyao, Yin Zifang, Mao Guangjun, Zhang Jinghong, Wang Kunyi, Cai Shengnan, Lü Yuzhai, Xu Jinbiao, Wang Runzhai, and Zhao Fengshan. (3) Before manufacturing new rickshaws, the Municipal Council should be notified. The 131 rickshaw owners who are required to replace their rickshaws with new ones should declare at this office this afternoon whether they have prepared new rickshaws themselves, and register the number of rickshaws for reference in order to determine the purchase and rush production. Resolved: Passed. (4) Old-style new rickshaw frames should be purchased by the cooperative. The purchase price is 18 yuan for oil-wood rickshaw bodies and 12 yuan for hemp-ticket rickshaw bodies. The selling price is 23 yuan for oil-wood rickshaw bodies and 18 yuan for hemp-ticket rickshaw bodies. Resolved: Passed. (5) The temporary cooperative fund, as decided by the preparatory meeting, will be 10 yuan per rickshaw. The first installment will be 5 yuan per rickshaw to cover the preparatory expenses (to be collected starting with the December donation). The second installment will be 2 yuan per rickshaw. From the third installment onwards, 1 yuan per rickshaw will be collected monthly until the total of 10 yuan is collected. Resolved: Passed. (6) Starting from December 3rd, rickshaw owners should collect the rickshaw puller registration application forms from the association and immediately introduce the rickshaw pullers to the registration offices in each district for registration. One rickshaw puller per rickshaw. According to the date of the rickshaw puller registration application form issued by the Municipal Council last month, the deadline will be extended by two weeks. Resolved: Passed. Furthermore, the Municipal Council's registration of rickshaw pullers has been extended by two weeks after negotiations with the rickshaw owners. The registration will be handled at 2 locations, Xinzha Road and Jiaxing Road, starting today.

The Municipal Council Sends Police Officers for Strict Inspection

Since the Public Concession Municipal Council began registering self-use rickshaw pullers, each registered rickshaw puller has been issued an armband with a white number on a blue enamel background, designated to be tied to the left arm for identification. Jiyuan Dharma Assembly Establishes a Porridge Kitchen

The Jiyuan Dharma Assembly on Avenue Road, in keeping with the compassionate spirit of the Buddha, established a shelter during the January 28th Shanghai Incident, housing thousands of displaced compatriots. After the war ended, they were provided with funds to return to their hometowns. They also hold annual winter relief efforts, establishing factories to provide porridge, benefiting many impoverished people. This autumn, they initiated a Liyang emergency relief effort, joining with various charity organizations and the Wuxi Red Swastika Society to raise more than 60,000 yuan, purchasing grain to distribute according to the number of family members. The disaster victims were able to survive. As the severe winter is approaching, it is difficult for the poor people of Shanghai to make a living. The southwest corner is a particularly concentrated area of laborers and coolies. The assembly will continue its old practice of establishing a porridge kitchen at the site of the Xieqiao Yongxi Church. It is reported that Assembly President Wang Yiting and Xu Qianlin have appointed Yu Yuanjue and Feng Liantang to expedite preparations and start the distribution earlier. It is planned to begin in early December. However, the assembly lacks funds, and it is hoped that people of good faith from all walks of life will provide strong support.

Telegraph Bureau's Xiaodongmen Receiving Office Relocated and Merged

Merged into the Nanshi Bund Post Office

Effective from the 3rd of this month

In order to facilitate the public and save public funds, the Ministry of Communications has ordered the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau in this port to implement postal and telegraphic integration, that is, all post offices have already accepted telegrams, which is convenient for all walks of life. Now, because there are many post offices near the Xiaodongmen Zhonghua Road receiving office, such as the Bund Post Office, Dananmen Post Office, and Sanpailou Post Office, it is already convenient for merchants to send telegrams. Therefore, it ordered to be cut and merged. According to the spokesperson of the bureau on Sichuan Road yesterday, the Xiaodongmen receiving office had already been ordered to be cut and merged. However, because many people in the Nanshi area sent telegrams there, suddenly withdrawing it would inevitably cause overcrowding in the Bund Post Office. Therefore, it negotiated with the post office to add equipment and install reporting machine circuits in the post office. It has now been completed, and from December 3rd, the Xiaodongmen office has been closed and announced to all sectors that if there are telegrams, they can be sent at the receiving office in the nearby Bund Post Office.

Maid Colludes with Criminals to Extort from Her Master

The Master Smokes Opium and is Extremely Terrified

2,000 Yuan Used to Settle the Matter

丨丨The defendant Xu Gang has been arrested丨丨

Huashan Chief Shang Wu and Detective Wang Youshan of the Huishi Police Department, along with Western Chief Yang, arrested a suspect named Xu Gang, a native of Shaoxing, at the rooftop garden of the Xinxin Company on Guizhou Road at approximately 9:00 PM the night before. He was suspected of using the name of Xu Qihu to gather accomplices to extort 2,000 yuan. He was taken to the police station for detention and sent to the 8th Criminal Court of the First Special Court the next morning to apply for detention. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, rose to present the case, saying that two months ago, Xu received information that a certain wealthy household with the surname of 　, located at No. 19 Baoqing Lane, Tianjin Road, Hongkou, was smoking opium. He immediately colluded with Li Agen, Feng Ahui, and others to go to the household to demand 2,000 yuan as a birthday gift, otherwise they would report it to the police. The master was terrified upon hearing this, so he was forced to write a check for 2,000 yuan and handed it over to the defendants. After obtaining the cash, they divided it up. The method of distribution was that Xu, Li, Feng, and two others named Jia and Yi each received 300 yuan, and the remaining 500 yuan was given to the maid of the household, because the information about the household's wealth and opium smoking was leaked to Jia and Yi by the maid, who then passed it on to Xu and the others. Therefore, after Xu was arrested at the Xinxin rooftop garden last night, he confessed to the previous events and stated that they had previously discussed and conspired at the Leyuan Teahouse on Jiujiang Road. The detectives obtained the confession and went to No. 19 Baoqing Lane to investigate. Because it was late at night, the household was already asleep and refused to open the door, so they did not enter. They now request that Xu be detained for investigation. Questioned by Xu Gang, he confessed, "I only heard Li Agen and the others talk about this matter, but I did not actually conspire with them. According to Li, the mother's brother of the certain surname came to Shanghai from his hometown and borrowed 30 yuan from him but was refused, so he planned to extort money. I was arrested because I was chatting about this matter outside." Judge Wu Yanqi verified　 and ordered Xu to be detained until Friday for further questioning.

The Son of a University Professor Behaves Absurdly

Pawning Clothes to Smoke Opium and Falsely Reporting a Robbery

Forging a Fake Note to Defraud His Father

Cao Yuanfu, the son of Cao Shuheng (52 years old this year), a native of Suzhou who is currently a professor at Jiaotong University, residing at No. 9, Lane 336, Route Frelupt, French Concession, is 24 years old this year. Although he once studied at a certain middle school, he recently dropped out and stayed at home, not engaging in honest work, wandering outside, associating with bad friends, and addicted to opium. He was once arrested and sent to court for punishment, but he did not repent. On the evening of the 30th of last month, Cao, accompanied by his friend Wu Baosheng (32 years old, from Shandong) who lived at No. 144 Xinglong Street, Dapuqiao, went to the thatched shed at No. 　 of Jiageng Lane, Rue Kin-Kiang where the family of a fellow named Ye Jiazhen (32 years old) was smoking red pills. Later, because neither of them had any money on them, they had no money to pay, and Ye refused to give them credit. Cao took off the clothes he was wearing and temporarily pawned them. Then Cao changed his mind and thought that the weather was cold, he was weak and thinly clothed, and he had no money to use. He had an idea and discussed with Wu and Ye that Cao would write a fake promissory note, stating that he borrowed 50 yuan from Wu　sheng, and asked Ye Jiazhen to act as a guarantor. After 　the fake promissory note, he asked Wu and Ye to go to his father, Cao Shuheng, to seek compensation. After obtaining the money, the three of them would divide it up. After completing this fake procedure, Cao went home to sleep. His father saw him wearing short clothes and asked him where his clothes were. Cao replied that he had been robbed on the road. His father asked why he had not reported it to the police since he had been robbed. At this point, Cao Yuanfu reported to the French police station that night, claiming that he had been robbed of his clothes on the street in Jiageng Lane at 4:00 AM. Detective Ni Jinrong, accompanied by Cao, investigated the scene and asked Cao what kind of robbers had robbed him. Cao pointed to his friends Wu Baosheng and Ye Jiazhen. The detective then arrested Wu and Ye at their addresses and found the clothes. Only then did it come to light that Cao had pawned his clothes to Ye because he had no money to smoke red pills. Later, he colluded to write a fake promissory note in an attempt to get money from his father. The detective reported the information to the police chief, accusing Cao of falsely reporting a robbery and colluding with Wu and Ye to forge a fake promissory note in an attempt to defraud. He ordered that Cao, Wu, and Ye be arrested and detained together. Yesterday, they were sent to the Special Court. The police lawyer filed a public prosecution according to law. Judge Sun Penghai conducted a trial at the 8th Criminal Court and immediately sentenced Cao Yuanfu to 40 days of detention for repeatedly smoking opium substitutes. Wu Baosheng and Ye Jiazhen were each sentenced to 20 days of detention for smoking opium substitutes. In addition, Ye was sentenced to three months of imprisonment for forcibly detaining the clothes as a warning. The remaining charges against the three defendants were dismissed.

Major Surgery Room Completed at Hongqiao Sanitarium

Since its opening, the Hongqiao Sanitarium in western Shanghai has strived for perfection in various medical facilities. Its major surgery room has now been completed. It is divided into a steam sterilization room, a changing room, an equipment room, and a waiting room, which is connected to the west side of the surgery room, making it more convenient to use. The surgery room has air-conditioning and heating equipment, so the indoor temperature can be adjusted according to the change of seasons. The entire room uses a rubber floor, which can eliminate disturbing sound waves. The surroundings of the room are a very quiet green, with yellow tiles that do not reflect light, which can avoid glare. When performing eye, nose, ear, and throat surgery, there is also black light equipment. The lighting method adopted is a Zeiss reflector lamp without shadows. Regardless of the position, surgery can be performed on the operating table. It is now being used skillfully. In the past month, more than a dozen major surgeries, including cesarean sections, have been performed in the hospital, and the results have been excellent. Doctors and patients alike have found it very convenient.

Three Ring Brand Products Sell Well at Home and Abroad

In recent years, there has been a general trend in our country's clothing reform towards simplicity. The fundamental purpose of clothing is to be lightweight, warm, and comfortable. As a result, imports of wool clothing and fabrics amount to over 4.4 million yuan annually, which is deeply regrettable. It is found that the Lianhua Wool Weaving Factory, located in Hele Lane, North Henan Road, Shanghai, was established in the twelfth year of the Republic of China. It has long produced "Three Ring" brand white wool Interlock men's and women's underwear, jacquard woolen sweaters, thick and thin wool scarves, wool men's and women's socks, swimwear, and other products, which have been popular throughout the country and are widely praised. Recently, with the cold weather and the arrival of frost, the factory's wool products, in addition to being shipped to other locations long ago, are also in short supply in Shanghai. Their spirit of fighting against foreign goods is highly commendable. Recently, the factory's manager, Mr. Chen Zuogan, has further dispatched personnel to supervise all staff to rush to fulfill a large order of Interlock underwear for a certain warship anchored in the Huangpu River, which shows that the factory's products are excellent and its business is thriving, truly a good phenomenon in the advocacy of domestic goods. This reporter hopes that the factory will increase production and strive for excellence, to reverse the outflow of our country's wool clothing and fabric imports. It is also heard that the factory's latest 1935 style swimwear samples have been produced and will be rushed into production soon.

The Resignation of Cao Tonglu, Chief of the Second District of Shanghai County

The original second district of Shanghai County consisted of the old boundaries of Caoxing and Tangwan townships. Since the establishment of the municipal government and the division of the city and county, the two townships were merged into the second district, a district office was set up, and a district chief was appointed to manage local affairs. This summer, the former district chief, Ding Jiren, resigned due to illness, and it was difficult to find a replacement for a time, so Assistant Li Youtian temporarily took over. Recently, County Magistrate Pan, in view of the importance of district administration, specially selected Mr. Cao Tonglu to take over as district chief in accordance with the rules for the selection of district chiefs, and submitted a request to the Department of Civil Affairs for approval. Now, Instruction No. 10967 from the Department of Civil Affairs states, "The vacancy of the district chief of the second district of the county is now filled by Cao Tonglu. You are to appoint him to act as an agent and report the date of appointment for investigation." Mr. Cao, considering the complexity of district administration and his inability to bear the heavy responsibility, submitted his resignation by mail yesterday. The resignation is excerpted below: "I hereby submit a request to resign from the position of acting district chief of the second district due to my shallow talent and lack of reputation. I am untalented and unexpectedly received this honor, which has flattered me. I have studied since childhood and engaged in business after adulthood, having been away from my hometown for a long time and lacking credibility. I am neither familiar with the affairs of the people nor knowledgeable about worldly matters. Although the position of district chief is small, it concerns the people directly. It requires both the ability to manage the world and the talent to promote benefits and eliminate abuses. Mercy and might must be combined to meet the expectations of the honorable county magistrate and to gain the trust of the people of the entire district. I believe that my humble talents are utterly inadequate to cope with the situation. Rather than occupying the position in the future, it is better to give way today. I hereby submit this request to your honorable county magistrate to approve my resignation from the position of acting district chief of the second district and to select someone virtuous and capable to assist in district administration. This would not only be fortunate for me alone but would also bring happiness to the entire district. My sincere heart hopes for a clear understanding. I am extremely apprehensive as I await your orders. Respectfully submitted."

Further Investigation is Needed

The Hearing will be Rescheduled for Further Inquiry

Misdialed Mechanism Causes Guard Corps Member to be Shot

Gu A'xiang, a 24-year-old native of Anting, who lives at 86 Chongde Lane, Hengfeng Road, Zhabei, is a member of the Third Platoon of the Eighth Team of the Shanghai North District Guard Corps on Guangzhao Road. As the winter defense began, each member went on duty as usual. Yesterday evening, Gu returned home after completing his duties and unloaded his self-provided pistol, removing the bullets. Unexpectedly, there was still one bullet in the barrel. Because Gu A'xiang misdialed the mechanism, there was a sudden bang, and the bullet left the barrel, hitting his left leg, causing profuse bleeding. Employee Embezzlement Case of Automobile Company Reopens

Zhang Hesheng, Gu Songqiao and other employees of the Huxiang Automobile Company embezzled more than 230 yuan of public funds and instructed accountant Wu Ciyin to register it as public relations expenses for the Public Security Bureau. The Public Works Bureau discovered this and sent it to the Public Security Bureau for transfer to the local court. Prosecutor Xiao thoroughly investigated and prosecuted the case in the Criminal Court. Judge Sun Jikang held a public hearing once, the details of which have been recorded in previous reports. This case was again heard in the Fifth Court by Judge Sun yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, ordering Zhang Hesheng and Zhang Songqiao, who were in custody, to be brought to court. According to their confessions, the money and account books were managed by Chief Accountant Wu Ciyin, and they requested a thorough investigation. Next, the witness Gu Liangru testified, "I am 40 years old and from Jiading. I asked the Deputy Manager of the company, 'Who manages the money at the Shanghai Station?' He replied, 'Ni Guangyao.' I asked, 'When did the automobile company open?' He replied, 'June 1st.' I asked, 'What kind of account books does the automobile company use?' He replied, 'We used Chinese account books first, and then switched to foreign books.' I asked, 'Where are the previous account books?' He replied, 'At Wu Ciyin's place.' I asked, 'What does Zhang Hesheng manage?' He replied, 'Repairing machines.'" Finally, Mr. Gao, the chairman of the company's board of directors, testified, "Wu Ciyin has gone to Suzhou for business, so I was instructed to come as a representative." The judge asked, "They said that the draft accounts are with Wu Ciyin, do you know about this?" He replied, "According to Manager Ni Guangyao, the draft accounts are at the Nanxiang Station." The judge then ordered Mr. Gao to present the draft accounts at the next hearing for further review. The defendants were taken back into custody.

Bestial Behavior of a Servant in a Westerner's Home

Fu Wu, a 34-year-old woman from Suzhou, works as an amah (nursemaid) in a Westerner's home at 69 Avenue Albert in the French Concession. She has a ten-year-old daughter named Jinbao, who accompanies her. During the day, Jinbao attends a small school on Rue Maughi. Xu Yanzhang, a 23-year-old man from Shandong, works as a servant in a Westerner's home at 17 Rue Macleod in Hongkou. Because he is acquainted with the head servant and other servants at 69 Avenue Albert, Xu often goes to 69 Avenue Albert to hang out or play mahjong. On the afternoon of the 30th of last month, at 4:30 PM, Xu, having finished his work and having nothing to do, went to 69 Avenue Albert again to play mahjong with the head servant and other servants. At 6:30 PM, the chimney of the Westerner's home suddenly caught fire, and the Westerner called the fire brigade. The head servant and other servants who were playing mahjong all rushed outside to watch the firefighting. Xu, seeing that the amah Fu Wu's daughter, Jinbao, was alone in the room, was suddenly overcome with lust. He broke into the room and picked up the girl, intending to rape her. He used his fingers to dig into the girl's lower body, causing her to be injured, scratched, and bleed. The girl cried out in pain, and Xu released her and fled. When Fu Wu found out that her daughter's lower body was bleeding and Xu had fled, she reported the case to the French police and sent the girl to the hospital for examination. Fortunately, the hymen was not broken, but the exterior was scratched by fingers. She was treated and Detective Zhang Shan of the baojia, together with detectives from the Huishan Police Station, arrested Xu at 17 Rue Macleod the next day and brought him to the case. Yesterday, he was escorted to the Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. Lawyer Yuan Jiahong of the police station explained the case, and then the plaintiff Fu Wu and her daughter appeared in court to recount the experience of being injured. The judge, considering that it concerned public morals, prohibited spectators. The defendant was defended by lawyer Wu Kaisheng. After the judge Cao Jun heard the case, he ordered that the hearing be rescheduled for further investigation. The defendant was returned to custody.

The Shanghai Citizens' Association Petitions the Legislative Yuan to Amend the Progressive Stamp Tax Law

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Association yesterday petitioned the Legislative Yuan of the National Government to amend the current stamp tax law to comply with public opinion, stating that the stamp tax law is not in line with commercial conditions and requesting that it be amended to protect commercial interests. The association stated that it received a letter from the Third Branch, which stated that it had read in the newspaper that the Legislative Yuan had recently passed a stamp tax plan that calculates the stamp tax on the most frequent items on the market, such as invoices and receipts, using a progressive method, which means that one cent must be added for every ten yuan. Upon hearing this, they were extremely shocked. It is found that stamp tax in Europe and the United States is a simple and light tax, but the regulations promulgated in our country in recent years are not only extremely harsh and cumbersome, but also easily lead to faults and severe penalties. Therefore, the mention of stamp tax is often criticized by the world. Recently, all industries have been declining, and commercial conditions have been deteriorating. The old stamp tax regulations have already caused great pain. However, our government officials have not alleviated the people's suffering but have instead increased the tax by tens or even dozens of times. With such heavy oppression, our people have no way to breathe, let alone survive. Moreover, this progressive method can only be handled by those who have studied accounting. Our country is backward, and society still retains the morbid state of centuries ago. Most stores are run by rural brokers who will be unable to cope with this brand-new stamp tax law. If they cannot cope, they will be punished. As a result, the government will mobilize tax officials and police, and the masses of people will be subject to the heavy burden of stamp tax, unable to escape. Therefore, they dare to represent the citizens of this district and directly petition, requesting that the situation be forwarded to the Legislative Yuan. They earnestly request that the suffering of the people be considered, that the newly established plan be withdrawn, and that the existing regulations be maintained to protect the people's livelihood and alleviate commercial difficulties. All of this was reported to the association. It is found that the points mentioned are not without merit. Moreover, since the new stamp tax law was promulgated, merchants in various places have felt inconvenienced and have filed petitions for amendment. In law, it is essential to suit public opinion. The progressive method stipulated in the new stamp tax law is not only harsh and detailed but also does not understand public opinion. It should be amended. It is appropriate to prepare a document and submit it to your honorable court for review, earnestly requesting that your request be approved, as it would be a great benefit. Respectfully submitted to Sun, President of the Legislative Yuan, by Wang Xiaolai, Zhang Yichen, and Wang Yansong, Standing Committee Members of the Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Association.

The Municipal Finance Bureau Considers the Request of Brokerage Firms to Change Regulations

Draft Processing Opinions Have Been Prepared

Submitted to the Municipal Government for Approval

The various brokerage associations in this city have reported in various newspapers that the brokerage commission has been restricted too low in the brokerage business regulations promulgated by the municipal government, and they have repeatedly requested that the stamp tax regulations be revised. According to the person in charge of the Municipal Finance Bureau, this case was previously ordered by the municipal government to be reviewed and discussed, and ten abridged versions of the various industry associations were forwarded by the municipal secretariat. After detailed review by the bureau, it was found that the statements made by the associations regarding the huge expenses of Shanghai brokerage firms and the fact that the brokerage commission limit of only 3% of the cargo price is insufficient to maintain operations are true. However, the brokerage commission limit specified in the Shanghai Brokerage Business Regulations is based on the third item of the method for organizing stamp tax decided at the National Finance Conference. Whether the limit can be changed has been submitted to the municipal government to be forwarded to the Ministry of Finance for review and handling to resolve the issue. Regarding the various points raised by the associations to amend the regulations, those that do not have a major impact on stamp tax revenue have also been adopted as much as possible to ensure that tax revenue and commercial conditions are considered simultaneously. Since the stamp tax is designated for education funds, the bureau will issue 42,000 yuan to the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office this year, so it cannot be changed.

Following the request, which affects the tax amount, the brokerage tax is an old local tax. The remaining articles of the Brokerage Business Regulations, as well as the commodity lists, etc., are all based on the original Jiangsu Provincial Brokerage Regulations, with reference to the drafting. There is no major change. Brokerage firms that have expired should pay taxes and exchange certificates in accordance with the regulations. Those that have not expired should apply for verification. Before the brokerage commission limit is determined, a request has been made to postpone the implementation of the promulgated regulations. As for the request from the various industry associations to change the brokerage certificates to be certified and collected by the associations, it is found that various taxes in this city have always been collected directly by the bureau's various tax collection offices as a principle. If various brokerage firms voluntarily guarantee and collect certificates through their industry associations, the bureau will not prohibit it. However, the various associations cannot force the various brokerage firms to entrust collection on their behalf. The entire case has now been prepared by the bureau with processing opinions and submitted to the municipal government for approval, and it should be resolved soon.

The Closing of the Improved Chinese Bookkeeping Exhibition Yesterday

15,000 Spectators Praised It Satisfied

Standard Account Tables and Documents Begin Distribution

The Improved Chinese Bookkeeping Exhibition, which opened on December 1 and continued for three days, closed yesterday. Among the three days, the number of visitors was the highest on the day before yesterday (Sunday), totaling more than 15,000 people, all of whom expressed satisfaction. This can be called an unprecedented grand occasion. A continuation of the various situations is recorded below.

A Special Room will be Opened to Display the Society's Public Exhibition: Yesterday was the last day, and there was still a considerable crowd of visitors. From morning to evening, there were approximately 5,000 people, especially in the afternoon. In addition to general business and accounting personnel, many groups of students from organizations and schools came to visit, such as the China Vocational School, the Zhijiang Vocational High School, the Wulun Vocational School, the Shanghai Provincial No. 3 Vocational School, the Shanghai Girls' High School, the Minli High School, and the Qingxin High School. The students were led by teachers and visited under the separate reception of important employees of the Xu Yongzuo Accounting Firm, who provided detailed explanations and distributed various printed materials. When reporters visited the association, they saw that most of the visitors at the various exhibition locations carefully reviewed the cases on display, attentively examining them. Some even took out paper and pens and copied down the organizational system of various accounting books and the classification contents of the accounts on the spot for reference after returning. This is because these materials are suitable for practical application, so they are considered treasures by those engaged in bookkeeping practice. It is heard that the association also plans to open a special room in the Xu Yongzuo Accounting Firm after the closing of the exhibition to continue displaying various materials so that those who were unable to visit the exhibition will not be disappointed.

Important Slogans Explained: In addition to the various accounting book examples, books, magazines, and charts and slogans mentioned in previous reports, the society's exhibition content also included many newly added accounting instructions and incisive slogans yesterday, which were hung in various places. Four are recorded below: (1) We advocate reforming Chinese bookkeeping based on China's inherent system, adopting the world's latest theories, and using the most economical and effective methods. (2) Chinese bookkeeping has a history of thousands of years and has its own value. How can we abandon it ourselves? (3) The advantages of Chinese bookkeeping are: 1. The theory is simple and clear; 2. The method is simple and convenient; 3. It is popular and easy to understand; 4. It saves expenses. The disadvantages are: 1. There is no fixed classification of accounts; 2. There is no fixed organization of accounting books; 3. There is no fixed format of account styles; 4. There are no fixed rules of accounting methods. Therefore, it is a pity to abandon it, and it is easier to improve it. (4) Improving Chinese bookkeeping must apply scientific methods, be based on accounting principles, seek to be practically applicable, and be premised on economic principles. As for whether the bookkeeping books and writing materials are domestic or foreign goods, whether the format of the accounting books is horizontal or vertical, and even whether the text and numbers used for bookkeeping are Chinese or Western, all of these are secondary issues and there are no insurmountable obstacles. We believe that if we want to use domestic paper and pens and take into account bookkeeping habits, we should continue to use the vertical format for registration. In the future, foreign paper and pens can be self-made, and if accounting personnel are accustomed to horizontal writing, they may also change to horizontal recording. As for the account theory and accounting methods of Chinese bookkeeping, they are simple, convenient, and in line with the concepts of Easterners, and they are easy for the general public to understand. We advocate maintaining this from beginning to end.

The Issuance of Standard Account Tables: The improved Chinese accounting book forms prepared by Xu Yongzuo Accounting Firm were printed and distributed by the Standard Document Manufacturing and Sales Office. All of these were displayed this time. It is heard that because of the good paper quality, solid binding, and lower prices than ordinary popular ones, all visitors considered them very economical and practical. These account book forms could have been ordered on the spot during the exhibition period. It is heard that a total of more than 200 companies have ordered them in recent days, which also shows the depth of the general merchants' trust in improved Chinese bookkeeping. It is now heard that the Standard Account Table Document Manufacturing and Sales Office has printed many exquisite samples. Anyone who attaches a two-cent stamp can request a copy. In addition to the Standard Account Table Document Manufacturing and Sales Office at 123 Avenue Edward VII, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Mechanized Domestic Goods Factory United Association, the New Sound News Agency, the World Book Company, the Datong Book Company, the Scientific Arts Equipment Hall, the Practical Science and Arts Hall, and the Modern Book Company are now selling them.

At the request of the various professions, it is also in accordance with the tax amount. In addition, the brokerage tax is an old local donation and tax. The remaining articles of the Brokerage Business Regulations, as well as the commodity lists, etc., are all based on the original Jiangsu Provincial Brokerage Regulations, with reference to the drafting, and there is no major change. Brokerage firms that have expired should pay taxes and exchange certificates in accordance with the regulations. Those that have not expired should apply for verification. Before the brokerage commission limit is determined, a request has been made to postpone the implementation of the promulgated regulations. As for the request from the various industry associations to change the brokerage certificates to be certified and collected by the associations, it is found that various taxes in this city have always been collected directly by the bureau's various tax collection offices as a principle. If various brokerage firms voluntarily guarantee and collect certificates through their industry associations, the bureau will not prohibit it. However, the various associations cannot force the various brokerage firms to entrust collection on their behalf. The entire case has now been prepared by the bureau with processing opinions and submitted to the municipal government for approval, and it should be resolved soon.

The Tax Affairs Department of the Ministry of Finance yesterday received Announcement No. 1 from the New Life Movement Committee of the Ministry of Finance, stating: "Only with a strong people can there be a strong country, and only with a healthy body can there be a healthy spirit. Therefore, strengthening the body has become a recognized and necessary matter to promote in the current trend. In our country, during the Three Dynasties, the Qin and Han dynasties, emphasis was placed on sports, and it was a common custom. The so-called 'Three times for farming, one time for military training' was the slogan of the Three Dynasties. Archery and chariot driving were given equal importance with rites and music, which was the custom during the Zhou and Qin dynasties. Civil affairs and military preparations were equally important, which was the habit during the two Han dynasties. These are all recorded in history and are clearly verifiable. Later, the rulers used ignorance to control the people, and the morale of the scholars declined. The teachings of Buddhism and Taoism flourished in the Wei, Jin, and Six Dynasties, and the system of science flourished in the Tang, Ming, and Qing dynasties. People buried themselves in books and stopped talking about military affairs, resulting in the weakening of the race and the slackening of all affairs. The name of 'sick man' became a common saying. Treading on frost leads to hard ice. Learning from the past will prevent future mistakes. We cannot have deep regret over the addition of adversity. There is a reason for this. Chairman Chiang promotes the New Life Movement, considering it an important tool for the revival of the nation. Propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame are marked as the goals, and new regulations are set for clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Special emphasis is placed on the improvement of sports. The people of the country are also gradually awakening and paying attention to it. This committee was established by order. In addition to strictly implementing the work plan outline promulgated by the general assembly, we now plan to promote sports, starting with 'netball' and 'national martial arts.' Comrade Deng Xian is recommended as the netball instructor, and Comrade Wang Zhijun is recommended as the national martial arts instructor. We will separately solicit members and organize practice. We hope that from now on, we can wash away the sickly appearance of pale faces and thin muscles and train hard men with bronze muscles and iron bones to shoulder arduous tasks and save the country from disaster. All my comrades should not lag behind. The registration locations and dates are as follows: (1) Each of the departments should separately solicit trainees for 'netball' and 'national martial arts' and submit a list to Wang Zhijun of the Taxation Department. (2) Please submit the lists within five days." It is heard that the department is also preparing to organize.

It is now scheduled for the main ceremony to be held at noon today, and then the coffin will be moved to the Tongru Chonghai Qi Five Counties Compatriot Association for temporary placement.

Obituary of Madam Wu

The late Madam Wu, mother of Wu Cheng-suo and Wu Cheng-zhu, passed away at 2 PM on December 2nd. The funeral will be held today (the 4th) at 9 AM at the Shanghai Funeral Home on Maple Forest Bridge, Xujiahui Road, with the encoffining ceremony at 10 AM and interment at the China Public Cemetery at the Wu Family Lane stop on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road. Madam Wu was diligent and thrifty in managing her household, skilled in educating her sons, and treated people with humility and sincerity. Her virtuous character was rarely seen in the world. Her eldest son, Wu Cheng-dong, is currently the Director and Factory Manager of the Taishan Brick and Tile Company. Her second son, Cheng-zhu, is an engineer at the Shanghai Wireless Telegraph General Station of the Ministry of Communications. He is deeply knowledgeable in wireless technology and has made significant contributions, a rare talent in the engineering field. Her eldest daughter, Wei-xian, is married to Li Songbao, who assists in managing tea businesses and exporting them abroad. Her second daughter, Shi, is married to Huang Shoumin, a prominent figure in the business world, currently the General Manager of Taishan Brick and Tile Company and the General Manager of Puyi Yarn Factory.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the area around Shandong is clear and cold, with strong winds from the northwest to the north. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River are clear and cold, with morning fog and winds from the north to northeast. The East China Sea and the Taiwan Strait are cloudy with localized rain, with strong seasonal winds from the north to northeast. The area around Southern Luzon and Macclesfield Bank is experiencing bad weather. The center of the first typhoon was within 60 miles of 16 degrees north latitude and 112 degrees east longitude at 6 AM, remaining stationary or moving very slowly. Wind force unknown. The center of the second typhoon was within 60 miles of 15 degrees north latitude and 124 degrees east longitude at 6 AM, moving northwest. Wind force unknown. Also, the temperature in Shanghai in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday was a high of 49.5 and a low of 29.8. On the same day last year, the high was 66.7 and the low was 38.3.

Incoming Article: China and the World Crisis (II)

Lecture by Dr. Eddy, Recorded by Bingxun Speedwriting Company, Shen Wan Speedwriter

Now we can divide those in power into four types of people: (1) those who are conservative, in advantageous positions, and standing at a special stage; (2) free thinkers, who want to improve the existing system and create new systems; (3) radicals, who want to overthrow all old systems to create a new one; (4) reactionaries, who want to maintain their special interests and therefore want to overthrow the radicals. I was born into a wealthy family, but I am not conservative, because I am dissatisfied with the existing system. Later, I became a free thinker, wanting to improve it, but I felt it was still not enough, so I became a radical, wanting to create a new system. Now I am a socialist. I advocate building a new system without bloodshed. I will give an example: I live near a central station, which is a very large station with fifty tracks and many trains coming and going, with a million people passing through every day. Many things are transported by train. This old station is very small, very dark, and very dirty. If we want to build a new station, millions of people would be inconvenienced, and the station cannot be built in a short time. It would take at least one or two years to complete. So, we temporarily maintain the status quo, build twenty-five tracks underground, and build new buildings around the old station. When the new buildings are completed, we will tear down the old station. This way, traffic will not be disrupted at all, and the people will not feel inconvenienced. So, if we want to create a new China, we must use this method. Now we know that these people are dissatisfied with the old system or the existing government. I also have many dissatisfactions with the American government, but a country must have a government. So, first, there must be a government, and political laws must be orderly; (2) there must be a good government; (3) an autonomous government, a government of the people, by the people, and for the people. This kind of government cannot be had immediately, just like rebuilding a central station, we must slowly use the old station as a new foundation. Do not do it like Soviet Russia, which lost a total of ten million lives during the war with the White Russians. I also do not want China to have another Taiping Heavenly Kingdom revolution, and I do not want China to have frequent revolutions. Now there are two things we must strive for: (1) improve the existing system; (2) create a new system. In thirty years, I have come to China nine times. China's current hope is greater than before. Although there are many things that are wrong and unsatisfactory, China has a new hope. A few days ago, I looked down from the plane and saw places of light and darkness. We must find ways to improve the dark places. China has many talented people, a large labor force, with four million people, accounting for a quarter of the world's population. Farmers have a history of four thousand years, are most able to endure hardship, and have a special talent for competing with locals, which is not the case with the 和 and Filipinos. Moreover, the Chinese are one of the three major races. When Westerners in ancient times did not wear clothes, Chinese people wore silk clothes. When the West had no culture, the Chinese had already invented the compass, paper, gunpowder, printing, etc. China is not only an ancient nation, but also a new nation, and it is a powerful nation. The Red Indians of the Americas are gradually disappearing, but 80% of Chinese farmers are able to endure hardship. Although the Mongol and Manchu races once conquered China, where is their power now? Because China built a moral foundation in ancient times, the Mongol and Manchu races, although strong, could not destroy the Chinese nation. I feel that Chinese people have a very good moral foundation. Today we have great hope. We see that China's recent construction of roads in various provinces is more effective than in Soviet Russia. Some buildings in Nanjing are better than those in 　斯科. China's young politicians are full of hope and willing to improve the countryside. They regard rural construction as their sacred duty. There is also a New Life Movement, advocated by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. This movement is a movement to build new morals, but it has not yet been fully successful. This movement promotes no longer exploiting the people and no longer taking advantage. China has a hopeful revelation, and China should build a new social order. Although China has hope, it also has dangers. Now China is suffering from international aggression. The four northeastern provinces have been lost, and North China is now in turmoil, filled with 乌烟瘴气. Japan is flooding North China with narcotic drugs such as heroin and morphine, like dark clouds in the sky. Now China must choose one of two paths: either like Poland, sinking into destruction, or like Denmark, saving itself. In the past, Poland had powerful enemies in the east, who seized the four eastern provinces, and the rest of the country was also in great danger. Their farmers were ignorant and uneducated, and their leaders were divided and fought each other, all with the aim of taking advantage. So, for one hundred and fifty years, there was no Poland on the map. If China continues to embrace this taking-advantage mentality, I am afraid that in one hundred and fifty years, there will be no China on the map either. We see that the destruction of Goryeo was also due to taking advantage. Provincial governors took advantage, the government took advantage, and the emperor exploited the people, so Goryeo was destroyed. Now the street names of Goryeo have been changed to Japanese names, and Japanese characters are being taught in Goryeo. So, the habit of taking advantage in China must be stopped. We hope that farmers will also receive proper education, just like in Denmark. At one time, Denmark was occupied by Germany. The fertile provinces in the south, its farmers, were ignorant, uneducated, and its leaders were divided, each doing their own thing, also taking advantage. Fortunately, two people later came out to save Denmark: one was a bishop, and the other was Mr. Yongde. What they did was: (1) awaken the people's patriotism; (2) revive education; (3) build rural areas, distribute land, so that 50% of the farmers have land to cultivate, lend money to farmers, and create cooperatives, better than Germany, Russia, and the United States; (4) use religion to improve national morals. Using the above four methods to change Denmark's bad system, other countries, such as England and Canada, have also implemented it. China can also implement it, and China can also recover the lost territories of the four northeastern provinces. Do we follow Poland or Denmark? To improve China, to unite China, just like Denmark. For this reason, I have returned to China again. (To be continued)

Ministry of Education Explains Educational Laws and Regulations Compendium

The following is a summary of recent interpretations of educational laws and regulations by the Ministry of Education: (1) Regarding the explanation that graduation certificates without affixed photographs should be invalid, an instruction was sent to the Shaanxi Education Department stating: Upon investigation, graduation certificates from secondary and higher education institutions should, in accordance with regulations, have a recent two-inch photograph of the graduate affixed. Those without affixed photographs should be deemed invalid. Furthermore, the regulations for school graduation and completion certificates have been revised by the Ministry into the Regulations for School Graduation Certificates, promulgated in June of last year and circulated for compliance. This is for your information. (2) Regarding the interpretation of the Regulations for Elementary Schools, an order was issued to the Fujian Education Department stating: Upon investigation, the "original salary" mentioned in Article 88 of the Regulations for Elementary Schools refers to the original salary grade received by teachers when applying for leave. Regardless of whether the school has reserve funds or whether it is separately provided by the educational administrative organ, the school should submit a request to the competent educational administrative organ for verification and handling. As for the years of service before the promulgation of the regulations, they may be calculated retroactively. This is for your information and for transmission to relevant parties.

Shandong Education Department Obeys Order to Resolve Qilu University President Issue

▲Already issued instructions to Qilu University and a letter to the Board of Directors

丨If necessary, the competent educational authority may reorganize it丨

(Jinan Express News) Students from the liberal arts and science departments of Shandong Private Qilu University previously launched a movement due to the president issue and the issue of student roster filing, and students repeatedly went to the provincial government Education Department to petition and request four things (see separate article). The Education Department then submitted the students' petition and requests to the Ministry of Education for review. During this period, the students once suspended classes due to the Western board of directors overturning the resolution and suspecting the school authorities of various wrongdoings, awaiting the vote of the entire board of directors on the 5th of this month. Yesterday, the Ministry of Education sent a telegram to the Education Department, ordering it to quickly instruct the board of directors to resolve the president issue, and citing the provisions of Article 19, paragraph 2 of the revised Regulations for Private Schools: the board of directors' selection of the president must be approved by the competent educational administrative organ; if the president is incompetent, they may be ordered to select another; if the person selected is still incompetent, the competent educational authority may temporarily appoint someone; if the board of directors is in dispute, it may be ordered to reorganize within a time limit. The Education Department has notified Qilu University and the board of directors. The letters and telegrams are copied below:

▲Instructions to Qilu University: The Ministry of Education's telegram has been received, stating: "The Qilu University Board of Directors has scheduled a meeting on December 5th and should be ordered to quickly resolve the president issue to restore the school's operations. The provisions of Article 15, paragraph 2 of the revised Regulations for Private Schools should be noted and the meeting's progress reported." Upon investigation, the original text of Article 19, paragraph 2 of the revised Regulations for Private Schools states: "Regarding school administration, the president or dean is fully responsible for the selection by the board of directors. The board of directors shall not directly participate. The selected president or dean shall be subject to the approval of the competent educational administrative organ. The board of directors may at any time re-elect the president or dean who has neglected their duties. The competent educational administrative organ may also order the board of directors to re-elect the president or dean who is deemed incompetent by the educational administrative organ. If the re-election is still incompetent, the competent educational administrative organ may temporarily appoint someone. When the board of directors has a dispute that causes a standstill, the competent educational administrative organ may order it to reorganize within a time limit. If necessary, the competent educational administrative organ may reorganize it." It is hereby ordered that the university be informed and pay close attention to this matter. This order.

▲Letter to the Qilu University Board of Directors: The students of the liberal arts and science departments of Private Qilu University previously petitioned the provincial government and this department multiple times due to the vacancy of the president and the lack of a person in charge, and suspended classes on the 26th of this month. All students went to the provincial government and this department twice to petition, submitting a petition with four requests: (1) Select a president; (2) Reorganize the board of directors; (3) Re-elect the dean of the medical school; (4) If the board of directors has the above intentions, it should report to the filing office three years in advance. They were told to return to school, resume classes, and await resolution. On the 24th, the director of this department personally went to the school to inspect it once. The next day after the suspension of classes, I returned to the school to convene teachers, staff, and student representatives to discuss the four opinions of the student representatives: (1) If the board of directors on December 5th has no results, who will be responsible for the recurrence of disputes? (2) If the board of directors cannot resolve the president issue and the student roster issue, please find a way to present it to the ministry. (3) The president selected by the board of directors must consider the demands of the students, that is, they must have the responsibility to develop the liberal arts and science departments and must not do anything detrimental to the liberal arts and science departments. (4) If students resume classes, they will rely on the government to obey government orders and resume classes. Please ask the director to maintain the school, except for the first item that is promised to be handled responsibly, and the fourth item is requested in person. The chairman of the board of directors, Vice Chairman Li, should cooperate with the staff and students to automatically resume classes. For the first item, because it is a dispute within the board of directors itself, if it cannot be resolved, the board of directors should be responsible. For the third item, sympathy is given in principle. The student side repeatedly stated that because they trust the government, they agree to resume classes immediately, but please the government side must do its best to urge the realization of its various requests. Upon investigation of this matter, Provincial Governor Han paid close attention to it and handed down the petition, ordering the department to quickly deal with it. The social aspect considers the school to be the highest institution of learning in this province and feels deeply serious about this matter. When your board of directors meets on December 5th, please pay special attention to the selection of the president and the student requests, and quickly resolve them. If the president issue still cannot be resolved at that time, and the school affairs are still not in charge, and thus another incident is brewed, the government side cannot be responsible. Please attach a copy of the petition and send it to your board of directors for review and careful handling. Sincerely, to the Board of Directors of Private Qilu University.

The principals of all large, medium, and small schools in the city discussed the matter of urgently raising donations for disaster areas. The Municipal Education Bureau convened a principals' meeting at the YMCA on Eight Immortals Bridge yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, and decided on the following principles:

Attending Principals: Those attending yesterday included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Section Chief Li Dachao, Municipal Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan, Section Chief Chen Bai, Standing Director of the Municipal Education Association Huang Zaoxiong, as well as principals of Guanghua, Fudan, Jinan, Daxia, Jingye, Wuben, Wusong, Aiguo, Huadong, Si Shang, Chengzhong, Peiming, Shangnv, Minguang, Guangzhao, Zhengxing, Junyi, Minli, Binhai, Wanzhu, He'an, Shangwen, Xicheng, Xinmin, Chongshi, Bide, and other schools, including Tao Guangzhou, Yan Zhenyu, Cheng Zheng, Chen Jicheng, Ma Jiazhen, Jin Tongzhang, Tang Zenghu, Huang Daping, Gu Yinqian, Xu Shushen, Yang Jingyi, Wang Dingcheng, Pan Dingyuan, and Shen Xibin, totaling over 500 people.

Chairman's Report: Director Pan, the chairman, first gave a report, stating that this year's natural disasters in various places are extremely serious, the rural economy is bankrupt, and the people's lives are difficult to maintain. Although Shanghai is affected by the economic downturn, it is still fortunate compared to the inland. Therefore, it is hoped that the citizens of Shanghai, regardless of all walks of life, should do their part to participate in the disaster relief donation campaign. Therefore, the mayor convened representatives from all walks of life to organize a general donation association, and decided to implement a general donation starting from the 8th. Before the 8th, all parties must have adequate preparations. The special invitation to all principals today is to discuss the fundraising methods of the education community, etc. Li Dachao then reported on the preparations for fundraising.

Principles Decided: The principals then discussed and decided on the following principles: (1) The Education Bureau will calculate the number of teachers and students in the city's large and medium-sized schools and send it to the General Office of the General Donation Association for the issuance of receipt books. (2) From the 5th to the 7th, each school should prepare a letter stamped with the school seal and send a person in charge to the General Office at the Sichuan Road YMCA to collect the receipt books. (3) All 10-cent, 20-cent, and 40-cent receipts will be calculated in silver dollars. (4) Elementary school students should donate 10 cents in silver dollars per person, middle school students 20 cents, university students 40 cents, and principals and teachers should donate at least one silver dollar per person. (5) Each school should submit the donations and donation books to the General Office before the 15th. (6) Schools that do not collect receipt books and do not submit donations within the specified time limit will have their names published in the newspaper by the General Office, announcing the collection of donation books and calling back donations. The discussion ended at around 4:00 PM.

Zhejiang Education Department Orders All Middle Schools to Improve Equipment

▲Purchase funds must absolutely not be used for other purposes

The Zhejiang Education Department, considering that various school equipment, such as books, instruments, samples, military training equipment, and sports equipment, are of great importance to school efficiency, in order to supervise and improve it, specifically ordered all secondary schools to comply with the expenses listed in the third item, "Purchase Funds," of each school's budget for this year, and to purchase equipment separately according to the actual needs of each school. Gansu College President Deng Zheming Comes to Shanghai for Inspection

They have visited Tongji and Fudan Universities separately since yesterday. In order to understand the educational situation in Gansu Province, the reporter visited Deng at his residence yesterday. It happened that Deng was out. According to Zhu, Gansu Province is located in the Northwest, and various undertakings are inferior to those in the Southeast provinces. The province's education is of course not as good as Jiangsu Province. There are only more than 1,340 primary schools in the province, and there are more than 900,000 school-age children in the province. There are a total of 32 public and private middle schools with a total of more than 1,900 students. As for universities, there is only Gansu College, so Gansu College is the highest institution of learning in the Northwest. Only one college has been established in the five provinces of Gansu, Ningxia, Qinghai, Shaanxi, and Xinjiang. Now, in the midst of this construction of the Northwest, it is extremely important to improve the educational level of the Northwest. Zhu continued, the quantity of production in Gansu in recent years has improved compared with 1929, but it has not yet recovered to the situation before 1926.

Jiang Yuanxin Returns to China After Studying Abroad

▲Gained more insights into cooperative undertakings

Jiang Yuanxin, courtesy name Zuomin, is from Xiaoshan, Zhejiang. In the summer of 1925, he graduated from the Department of Economics of National Peking University. He immediately went south to participate in the National Revolution. During the Northern Expedition, he served in the General Political Department and once served as the director of the division's political department. In 1927-28, he served as a member of the executive committee of the Zhejiang Provincial Party Headquarters. In the autumn of 1929, he was the secretary of the Finance Department of the Zhejiang Provincial Government and concurrently the head of the First Section. He had detailed planning for the province's finances and made many achievements. In particular, the rectification of miscellaneous taxes, such as the unified tax, license tax, and brokerage tax at that time, all increased revenue sharply due to the elimination of embezzlement, which was an unprecedented initiative in the history of Zhejiang's finances. The Zhejiang Provincial Government praised his ability and sent him to the United States and other countries to study finance in order to deepen his knowledge. He went abroad in the summer of 1931, first to the United States, then to countries such as the United Kingdom, France, Germany, Russia, Switzerland, Denmark, and Italy. He carefully inspected everything he went to, without leaving any concerns, and gained the most from rural economics and cooperative undertakings. Therefore, domestic comrades urged him to return as soon as possible so that he could contribute to China's social construction. Jiang also believed that the investigation of several years could come to an end, so he took the Conte Rosso ship from Italy and returned to China, arriving in Shanghai late last night. At one time, there were many people who knew him from various places and went to the wharf to welcome him.

The Sports Referees Association is Recruiting New Basketball Referees

▲ Registration Begins Now, Exam on the 11th

The Shanghai Chinese Sports Referees Association will hold an exam for new basketball referees on December 11th (Tuesday) at the YMCA on Sichuan Road. Those who are interested and willing to serve the sports community can register at the YMCA Sports Department with Ling Xitao or at the National Sports Advancement Association with Zhou Jiaqi, starting now. Each person should submit a registration fee of one yuan and a deposit of four yuan (which will be refunded regardless of whether they pass or fail). The deadline is set for the 9th, and late applications will not be accepted. The exam will consist of a written test, an oral test, and a practical test. The first written test is the preliminary test. Those who pass the preliminary test will take the oral test and a visual acuity test. Those who pass both will then undergo a practical test to determine their acceptance.

Changshu Climbing Competition: Zhang Yiwei Reaches Yushan Peak First

▲ Female Student Zhao Yuqin Also Reaches the Finish Line

(Changshu Correspondence) In order to promote public sports, the Public Sports Field of this county has specially organized a climbing competition, with the Zushi Fushui Rock, the highest peak of Yushan, as the destination. The total height is 106 zhang (old chi), and the route starts from the old county field in the city, passes through Daonan Street, then through County West Street, Nanshi Center, Siqian Main Street, Zhao Alley, Huai Liu Lane, West Alley, North Gate Main Street, out of the North Gate, climbs up from Taojian, through Shiwujian, Weimo Pine Forest, Dou Niu Station, and reaches the entrance of the Zushi Temple at Fushui Rock as the finish line. The total length of the route is 5,575 meters, which is less than 10,000 meters, but it is indeed strenuous due to the mountain climbing. The Sports Field has been preparing for a month before everything was ready. The competition was held at 9:30 AM on the 2nd of this month, with a total of 100 participants, including one female, Zhao Yuqin, who bravely participated and attracted much attention from all walks of life. Therefore, in addition to the Education Bureau, the county magistrate, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and major businesses have donated more than 70 prizes. This time, not only students participated, but also rickshaw pullers, police officers, shop assistants, fire brigade members, and civil servants, which was quite enthusiastic and the interest was very strong. When the competition was held that morning, the streets along the route were blocked, which was unprecedented. Fortunately, all the police officers of the Public Security Bureau and the Boy Scouts of the 277th Regiment of the county high school maintained order along the way. When departing, 92 people actually reported, and 8 were absent. A total of 83 people were able to reach the finish line, which was a very good result. Zhang Yiwei took the lead from the very beginning, leading the way. Police officers Bian Zhiming, Xu Zhaoqi, and Lu Zugen also followed closely, never leaving his side. When passing the North Gate, Bian Zhiming once took the lead. Xu Zhaoqi was small and lively, but gradually fell behind due to his physical condition. When Zhang Yiwei reached the Tao Yuan Ravine, he suddenly used a trick to call out to Bian Zhiming, who was in front, saying that the journey ahead was still long and that he should proceed slowly, fearing that he would run out of energy in the end. Bian was eventually fooled by Zhang and proceeded shoulder to shoulder. When they reached Weimo and passed the pine forest, which was flat ground, Zhang immediately broke free and ran forward, and Bian was eventually abandoned. Therefore, Zhang Yiwei won the first place with a time of 29 minutes and 10 seconds. The second place was Chen Zancheng, who was about 30 to 40 meters away from the first one, with a time of 29 minutes, 21 seconds, and 3/5. The time was measured very accurately this time, because the mountaintop was equipped with a telephone for air defense, and the Security Team Leader was specially consulted to connect the telephone with the telephone at the issuing point. When the order was given to fire the gun, the gunshot could also be heard on the mountain telephone. The names and times of the top 15 are listed as follows:

(1) Zhang Yiwei, 29 minutes and 10 seconds; (2) Chen Zancheng, 29 minutes and 21.6 seconds; (3) Jin Genyuan, 29 minutes and 40 seconds; (4) Bian Zhiming, 30 minutes and 5 seconds; (5) Ma Haoqing, 30 minutes and 30 seconds; (6) Zhai Zhiping, 30 minutes and 55 seconds; (7) Tao Hongjun, 31 minutes and 11 seconds; (8) Xu Zhaoqi, 31 minutes and 12 seconds; (9) Jiang Yousi, 31 minutes and 12.4 seconds; (10) Gui Cheng, 31 minutes and 47 seconds; (11) Xie Hongfa, 31 minutes and 47.8 seconds; (12) Jiang Huaizu, 31 minutes and 50 seconds; (13) Lu Zugen, 32 minutes and 9 seconds; (14) Shen Shengsheng, 32 minutes and 14 seconds; (15) Ni Xisheng, 32 minutes and 14 seconds. The Sports Field has selected a total of 30 people, each receiving a silver cup and miscellaneous items. Although the female Zhao Qin was not selected, she received a gift for her promotion. Also, special prizes were given to the youngest Xu Zhaoqi (12 years old) and the oldest Wang Guoliang (41 years old).

Spring and Autumn

Little West Heaven

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 5: Laughing and Fawning, Raising Lanterns to Illuminate Careworn Faces, Driven by Empty Stomachs, Learning to Be Sophisticated with Makeup

Yueying, who was in the same predicament, laughed: Auntie is getting flustered. Didn't you roll up your clothes and use them as a pillow? Mrs. Hu exclaimed and scrambled to put on her clothes. While buttoning, she fumbled to open the front door. In the darkness, she saw a figure standing abruptly at the door. Even though she knew it was Little Ji, her heart was pounding a bit, and she took two steps back. Little Ji said: Is that Mrs. Hu? Mrs. Hu said: What's the rush, coming to find me in the dark? Little Ji said: I've spoken to that Master Jia, and we've arranged for you to bring someone to talk to him tomorrow morning. Mrs. Hu said: Did he say he'd give me a dollar? Little Ji said: That was just something I said to trick you into getting up. Mrs. Hu spat and tried to shut the door. Little Ji said: You must go. The dollar has already been given to me. Mrs. Hu said: Really? Give me the money. Little Ji hesitated for a moment and laughed: You don't trust me, and I don't trust you either. You go with someone tomorrow morning, and I'll naturally give it to you. Having said that, Little Ji turned and left. In his heart, he thought: A fisherman has to use some bait, and a chicken thief has to scatter some grain. So, he'll just spend a dollar. Since he's willing to spend a dollar, he doesn't have to worry about Mrs. Hu not coming. Little Ji returned to Little West Heaven with great confidence, preparing some things for the next day. Sure enough, at a little after six o'clock the next morning, Mrs. Hu brought Yueying quietly to the outside of Little Ji's room, first coughing softly twice. Little Ji was sitting in the room smoking paper cigarettes, looking at the ceiling and thinking about something. He clearly heard it but ignored it. Mrs. Hu had no choice but to hold onto the door and stick her head in, laughing: Brother Ji is in the room, why aren't you paying attention to me? Little Ji laughed: I can't see through walls. If you don't call me from outside, how would I know you've come? She held onto the door and walked in, whispering: Didn't you tell me to come in the morning? I'm here now. Little Ji said: Where's the girl? (80)

Friends

— Ji Chengxing

In this society where morality is declining and people's hearts are deteriorating, trying to find a few friends who share joys and sorrows with you is a difficult task. But trying to make friends who are only there for the good times is as easy as finding a needle in a haystack!

People nowadays value power and influence over friendship and loyalty because power and influence benefit them and give them opportunities to climb the social ladder. Perhaps everyone is used to seeing Old Zhang get lucky and become a high-ranking official, so Old Zhang's friends can find shelter under his big tree! Old Li made a fortune, and many friends chase after Old Li, waiting for his commands!

A person who is down on their luck is like a stinking crow, not even ants will come to smell it. I have never heard of a fallen nobleman being loved by a young woman, nor have I heard of a poor man being favored by a rich person. But I have heard of friendships breaking down because of a loss of financial control, and I have also heard of many people arguing over the amount of gifts their friends give them. They don't know what Fuller said: "Don't use gifts to make friends. When you stop giving, they will abandon you." Truly, people who alleviate the burdens of others in this world are rare, even if there are, they are like flowers in the desert!

"If there are no friends, it's truly lonely. The light of friendship is warm, without it, the end of humanity seems near!" I often think like this.

"Even if that person has committed a crime of theft, as long as he has a precious friendship with his friends, he is still kind and approachable!" One of my friends said.

Do humans really not need friends? If they don't, then please read this famous quote from Stevenson: "One day we love another, we should serve that person for one day. One day we are loved by another, I dare say we are indispensable for one day. One who still has a friend is not a useless waste."

▲Thought is like barren land. Without cultivation and nurturing, it will never bloom with brilliant flowers.

Miss Zhang

— Zhao Yongmei

I am quite fortunate to have been neighbors with Miss Zhang for a year and six months. According to Mrs. Liu, the neighbor, when Miss Zhang moved here, she was still wearing blue bamboo cloth clothes and cloth-soled shoes. Over the years, her attitude has changed greatly!

Indeed, Miss Zhang is beautiful now. She has curly, fine hair, large, dark eyes, a delicate face like powder, and cherry lips like blood. Adding high-heeled shoes and a long cheongsam, she appears extraordinarily beautiful. In short, she has all the modern decorations of a modern woman. It would be a great injustice to say that she is not the standard beauty of East Asia.

Movies seem to be her destiny from a previous life. When "Song of the Fishermen" was screened for sixty consecutive days, she was like "Song of the Fishermen," never missing a session. When she came back after watching the movie, she praised the male movie stars as having artistic talent, but as for the female stars, she really didn't think much of them. If you chime in and say, "Miss Zhang, you are the best woman in the world!" Then she would smile sweetly and happily brew the finest and most fragrant tea buds for you.

Of course, Miss Zhang is educated. Singing and dancing are her specialties. After dinner or late at night, you can hear her singing the most popular song "Peach Blossom River is a Den of Beauties." Hearing this clear and beautiful song in boredom, I rejoice that my ears are so lucky.

Miss Zhang is a great talker. Whether it's the smallest fly or the vastness of the universe, once it's on her lips, she can explain it logically. It's a pity she's not a lawyer. If she were, I think she would be several times more popular than Zheng Yuxiu.

Miss Zhang doesn't care about spending money. She often says: What's so special about money? She spends an unknown amount on silk stockings and cosmetics every month. However, Miss Zhang's family is quite poor.

Not to Slacken the Slightest

Fragrant Misty Records of the Imperial Palace

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

"Ah! How handsome and magnificent he is!"

"With such a dignified and noble demeanor, he is worthy of being the monarch of a great country!"

After seeing this portrait, everyone couldn't help but admire it in secret. I think if the artist of this portrait did not specially enhance and embellish him because he was an emperor, then Qianlong's appearance can be said to be handsome and heroic, rarely seen in the world! But according to the words and deeds of this wise ruler recorded in official history and private biographies, we can easily believe that the portrait did not go beyond the scope of reality.

Qianlong in the painting is in the scene of hunting, riding a snow-white horse under his crotch, its spiritedness and magnificence, just enough to match its master's appearance. On the back of the horse, as usual, there is a saddle; this saddle is purely Mongolian style, with countless jewels inlaid on it. The two stirrups are all gold, shining brightly in the painting. Qianlong sits like a small mountain on this extremely luxurious saddle. Looking at him, he is also wearing a full hunting suit, covered with a apricot-yellow tight-fitting vest. A wide satin belt is tied around his waist, also yellow, with many beads nailed on it. His soft helmet is even more unique. The helmet itself is a pointed hat, but there are two ears hanging down on both sides, connected under the jaw, much like the format of the leather hats worn by airplane pilots today. The material of this hat is yellow satin, with a long and beautiful red tassel on top, all the way down to the edge of the hat. (190)

Nursery

Social welfare undertakings seem to have not yet been fully developed in China, so some have not yet been held, such as nurseries. In Soviet Russia, they are run strictly and well, but in China, the achievements have not yet made special contributions.
